<p><b><a href="/wiki/Modern_pentathlon" title="Modern pentathlon">Modern pentathlon</a></b> was first contested at the <a href="/wiki/Olympic_Games" title="Olympic Games">Olympic Games</a> at the <b><a href="/wiki/1912_Summer_Olympics" title="1912 Summer Olympics">1912 Summer Olympics</a></b> in <a href="/wiki/Stockholm" title="Stockholm">Stockholm</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sports-reference_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-sports-reference-1">[1]</a></sup> The sport was invented by Baron <a href="/wiki/Pierre_de_Coubertin" title="Pierre de Coubertin">Pierre de Coubertin</a>, the founder of the modern <a href="/wiki/Olympic_Games" title="Olympic Games">Olympic Games</a>.</p>
<p></p>
